Sets mouse options \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{\$newmask int }} Mouse mask options can be set with the following predefined constants\+: 

N\+C\+U\+R\+S\+E\+S\+\_\+\+B\+U\+T\+T\+O\+N1\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+S\+ED

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This will be set to the previous value of the mouse event mask.

int a mask to indicated which of the in parameter newmask specified mouse events can be reported. On complete failure, it returns 0.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily ncurses\+\_\+slk\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$format }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Initializes soft label key functions \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{\$format int }} If ncurses\+\_\+initscr eventually uses a line from stdscr to emulate the soft labels, then this parameter determines how the labels are arranged of the screen. 

0 indicates a 3-\/2-\/3 arrangement of the labels, 1 indicates a 4-\/4 arrangement and 2 indicates the PC like 4-\/4-\/4 mode, but in addition an index line will be created.
